func (dec *Decoder) tokenPrepareForDecode() error {
	// peek is only called when using the Token API.
	switch dec.tokenState {
	case tokenArrayComma:
		dec.tokenState = tokenArrayValue
	case tokenObjectColon:
		dec.tokenState = tokenObjectValue
func (dec *Decoder) tokenValueAllowed() bool {
	switch dec.tokenState {
	case tokenTopValue, tokenArrayStart, tokenArrayValue, tokenObjectValue:
func (dec *Decoder) tokenValueEnd() {
	switch dec.tokenState {
	case tokenArrayStart, tokenArrayValue:
		dec.tokenState = tokenArrayComma
	case tokenObjectValue:
		dec.tokenState = tokenObjectComma
func (dec *Decoder) Token() (Token, error) {
			if !dec.tokenValueAllowed() {
				return dec.tokenError(c)
			dec.tokenStack = append(dec.tokenStack, dec.tokenState)
			dec.tokenState = tokenArrayStart
			if dec.tokenState != tokenArrayStart && dec.tokenState != tokenArrayComma {
				return dec.tokenError(c)
			dec.tokenState = dec.tokenStack[len(dec.tokenStack)-1]
			dec.tokenStack = dec.tokenStack[:len(dec.tokenStack)-1]
			dec.tokenValueEnd()
			if !dec.tokenValueAllowed() {
				return dec.tokenError(c)
			dec.tokenStack = append(dec.tokenStack, dec.tokenState)
			dec.tokenState = tokenObjectStart
			if dec.tokenState != tokenObjectStart && dec.tokenState != tokenObjectComma {
				return dec.tokenError(c)
			dec.tokenState = dec.tokenStack[len(dec.tokenStack)-1]
			dec.tokenStack = dec.tokenStack[:len(dec.tokenStack)-1]
			dec.tokenValueEnd()
			if dec.tokenState != tokenObjectColon {
				return dec.tokenError(c)
			dec.tokenState = tokenObjectValue
			if dec.tokenState == tokenArrayComma {
				dec.tokenState = tokenArrayValue
			if dec.tokenState == tokenObjectComma {
				dec.tokenState = tokenObjectKey
			return dec.tokenError(c)
			if dec.tokenState == tokenObjectStart || dec.tokenState == tokenObjectKey {
				old := dec.tokenState
				dec.tokenState = tokenTopValue
				dec.tokenState = old
				dec.tokenState = tokenObjectColon
			if !dec.tokenValueAllowed() {
				return dec.tokenError(c)

== /home/umid/.sliver/go/src/encoding/json/jsontext/token.go ==
	invalidTokenPanic = "invalid jsontext.Token; it has been voided by a subsequent json.Decoder call"
var errInvalidToken = errors.New("invalid jsontext.Token")
type Token struct {
	// Tokens can exist in either a "raw" or an "exact" form.
	// Tokens produced by the Decoder are in the "raw" form.
	// Tokens returned by constructors are usually in the "exact" form.
	// The Encoder accepts Tokens in either the "raw" or "exact" form.
	// The following chart shows the possible values for each Token type:
	//	║ Token type      ║ raw field  │ str field  │ num field  ║
	//   - For tokens stored in "raw" form, the num field contains the
	Null  Token = rawToken("null")
	False Token = rawToken("false")
	True  Token = rawToken("true")
	BeginObject Token = rawToken("{")
	EndObject   Token = rawToken("}")
	BeginArray  Token = rawToken("[")
	EndArray    Token = rawToken("]")
	zeroString Token = rawToken(`""`)
	zeroNumber Token = rawToken(`0`)
	nanString  Token = String("NaN")
	pinfString Token = String("Infinity")

func hasToken(v, token string) bool {
	if len(token) > len(v) || token == "" {
	if v == token {
	for sp := 0; sp <= len(v)-len(token); sp++ {
		// The token is ASCII, so checking only a single byte
		if b := v[sp]; b != token[0] && b|0x20 != token[0] {
		// Check that start pos is on a valid token boundary.
		if sp > 0 && !isTokenBoundary(v[sp-1]) {
		// Check that end pos is on a valid token boundary.
		if endPos := sp + len(token); endPos != len(v) && !isTokenBoundary(v[endPos]) {
		if ascii.EqualFold(v[sp:sp+len(token)], token) {

func (up *socksUsernamePassword) Authenticate(ctx context.Context, rw io.ReadWriter, auth socksAuthMethod) error {
	case socksAuthMethodUsernamePassword:
		if len(up.Username) == 0 || len(up.Username) > 255 || len(up.Password) > 255 {

		b := []byte{socksauthUsernamePasswordVersion}
		b = append(b, byte(len(up.Password)))
		b = append(b, up.Password...)
		if b[0] != socksauthUsernamePasswordVersion {
			return errors.New("invalid username/password version")
			return errors.New("username/password authentication failed")

func (s *Scanner) switch2(tok0, tok1 token.Token) token.Token {
func (s *Scanner) switch3(tok0, tok1 token.Token, ch2 rune, tok2 token.Token) token.Token {

func (s *Scanner) Scan() (pos token.Pos, tok token.Token, lit string) {
		// Return artificial ';' token after /*...*/ comment
		pos, tok, lit = s.nlPos, token.SEMICOLON, "\n"
		s.nlPos = token.NoPos
	// current token start
	// determine token value
			tok = token.Lookup(lit)
			case token.IDENT, token.BREAK, token.CONTINUE, token.FALLTHROUGH, token.RETURN:
			tok = token.IDENT
				return pos, token.SEMICOLON, "\n"
			tok = token.EOF
			return pos, token.SEMICOLON, "\n"
			tok = token.STRING
			tok = token.CHAR
			tok = token.STRING
			tok = s.switch2(token.COLON, token.DEFINE)
			tok = token.PERIOD
				tok = token.ELLIPSIS
			tok = token.COMMA
			tok = token.SEMICOLON
			tok = token.LPAREN
			tok = token.RPAREN
			tok = token.LBRACK
			tok = token.RBRACK
			tok = token.LBRACE
			tok = token.RBRACE
			tok = s.switch3(token.ADD, token.ADD_ASSIGN, '+', token.INC)
			if tok == token.INC {
			tok = s.switch3(token.SUB, token.SUB_ASSIGN, '-', token.DEC)
			if tok == token.DEC {
			tok = s.switch2(token.MUL, token.MUL_ASSIGN)
				tok = token.COMMENT
				tok = s.switch2(token.QUO, token.QUO_ASSIGN)
			tok = s.switch2(token.REM, token.REM_ASSIGN)
			tok = s.switch2(token.XOR, token.XOR_ASSIGN)
				tok = token.ARROW
				tok = s.switch4(token.LSS, token.LEQ, '<', token.SHL, token.SHL_ASSIGN)
			tok = s.switch4(token.GTR, token.GEQ, '>', token.SHR, token.SHR_ASSIGN)
			tok = s.switch2(token.ASSIGN, token.EQL)
			tok = s.switch2(token.NOT, token.NEQ)
				tok = s.switch2(token.AND_NOT, token.AND_NOT_ASSIGN)
				tok = s.switch3(token.AND, token.AND_ASSIGN, '&', token.LAND)
			tok = s.switch3(token.OR, token.OR_ASSIGN, '|', token.LOR)
			tok = token.TILDE
			tok = token.ILLEGAL

type ContextToken interface {
CREDENTIAL MANAGEMENT
GSS_Acquire_cred             acquire credentials for use
GSS_Release_cred             release credentials after use
GSS_Inquire_cred             display information about credentials
GSS_Add_cred                 construct credentials incrementally
GSS_Inquire_cred_by_mech     display per-mechanism credential information
GSS_Process_context_token    process received control token on context
GSS_Wrap_size_limit          determine GSS_Wrap token size limit
GSS_GetMIC                   apply integrity check, receive as token separate from message
GSS_VerifyMIC                validate integrity check token along with message
	AcquireCred() error                                               // acquire credentials for use (eg. AS exchange for KRB5)
	InitSecContext() (ContextToken, error)                            // initiate outbound security context (eg TGS exchange builds AP_REQ to go into ContextToken to send to service)
	AcceptSecContext(ct ContextToken) (bool, context.Context, Status) // service verifies the token server side to establish a context
	MIC() MICToken                                                    // apply integrity check, receive as token separate from message
	VerifyMIC(mt MICToken) (bool, error)                              // validate integrity check token along with message
	Wrap(msg []byte) WrapToken                                        // sign, optionally encrypt, encapsulate
	Unwrap(wt WrapToken) []byte                                       // decapsulate, decrypt if needed, validate integrity check
		str = "token had invalid integrity check"

		str = "expired credentials detected"

	case StatusDefectiveToken:

type ContextToken interface {
CREDENTIAL MANAGEMENT
GSS_Acquire_cred             acquire credentials for use
GSS_Release_cred             release credentials after use
GSS_Inquire_cred             display information about credentials
GSS_Add_cred                 construct credentials incrementally
GSS_Inquire_cred_by_mech     display per-mechanism credential information
GSS_Process_context_token    process received control token on context
GSS_Wrap_size_limit          determine GSS_Wrap token size limit
GSS_GetMIC                   apply integrity check, receive as token separate from message
GSS_VerifyMIC                validate integrity check token along with message
	AcquireCred() error                                               // acquire credentials for use (eg. AS exchange for KRB5)
	InitSecContext() (ContextToken, error)                            // initiate outbound security context (eg TGS exchange builds AP_REQ to go into ContextToken to send to service)
	AcceptSecContext(ct ContextToken) (bool, context.Context, Status) // service verifies the token server side to establish a context
	MIC() MICToken                                                    // apply integrity check, receive as token separate from message
	VerifyMIC(mt MICToken) (bool, error)                              // validate integrity check token along with message
	Wrap(msg []byte) WrapToken                                        // sign, optionally encrypt, encapsulate
	Unwrap(wt WrapToken) []byte                                       // decapsulate, decrypt if needed, validate integrity check
		str = "token had invalid integrity check"
	case StatusCredentialsExpired:
		str = "expired credentials detected"
	case StatusDefectiveCredential:
		str = "defective credential detected"
	case StatusDefectiveToken:
		str = "defective token detected"
		str = "no valid credentials provided"
		str = "duplicate credential element requested"
	case StatusDuplicateToken:
		str = "duplicate per-message token detected"
	case StatusOldToken:
		str = "timed-out per-message token detected"
	case StatusUnseqToken:
		str = "reordered (early) per-message token detected"
	case StatusGapToken:
		str = "skipped predecessor token(s) detected"

func StringToKeyIter(secret, salt string, iterations int64, e etype.EType) ([]byte, error) {
	tkey := e.RandomToKey(StringToPBKDF2(secret, salt, iterations, e))

type SPNEGOToken struct {
	NegTokenInit NegTokenInit
	NegTokenResp NegTokenResp
func (s *SPNEGOToken) Marshal() ([]byte, error) {
		tb, err := s.NegTokenInit.Marshal()
			return b, fmt.Errorf("could not marshal NegTokenInit: %v", err)
		b, err := s.NegTokenResp.Marshal()
			return b, fmt.Errorf("could not marshal NegTokenResp: %v", err)
	return b, errors.New("SPNEGO cannot be marshalled. It contains neither a NegTokenInit or NegTokenResp")
func (s *SPNEGOToken) Unmarshal(b []byte) error {
		// Not a NegTokenResp/Targ could be a NegTokenInit
			return fmt.Errorf("not a valid SPNEGO token: %v", err)
		// Could be a NegTokenResp/Targ
	_, nt, err := UnmarshalNegToken(r)
	case NegTokenInit:
		s.NegTokenInit = v
		s.NegTokenInit.settings = s.settings
	case NegTokenResp:
		s.NegTokenResp = v
		s.NegTokenResp.settings = s.settings
		return errors.New("unknown choice type for NegotiationToken")
func (s *SPNEGOToken) Verify() (bool, gssapi.Status) {
		return false, gssapi.Status{Code: gssapi.StatusDefectiveToken, Message: "invalid SPNEGO token, unclear if NegTokenInit or NegTokenResp"}
		s.NegTokenInit.settings = s.settings
		ok, status := s.NegTokenInit.Verify()
			s.context = s.NegTokenInit.Context()
		s.NegTokenResp.settings = s.settings
		ok, status := s.NegTokenResp.Verify()
			s.context = s.NegTokenResp.Context()
	return false, gssapi.Status{Code: gssapi.StatusFailure, Message: "unable to verify SPNEGO token"}

type Token struct {
    Type  TokenType
type Tokens []Token
type TokenType rune
    // Single-character tokens are represented by their own character, for
    TokenOBrace   TokenType = '{'
    TokenCBrace   TokenType = '}'
    TokenOBrack   TokenType = '['
    TokenCBrack   TokenType = ']'
    TokenOParen   TokenType = '('
    TokenCParen   TokenType = ')'
    TokenOQuote   TokenType = '«'
    TokenCQuote   TokenType = '»'
    TokenOHeredoc TokenType = 'H'
    TokenCHeredoc TokenType = 'h'
    TokenStar    TokenType = '*'
    TokenSlash   TokenType = '/'
    TokenPlus    TokenType = '+'
    TokenMinus   TokenType = '-'
    TokenPercent TokenType = '%'
    TokenEqual         TokenType = '='
    TokenEqualOp       TokenType = '≔'
    TokenNotEqual      TokenType = '≠'
    TokenLessThan      TokenType = '<'
    TokenLessThanEq    TokenType = '≤'
    TokenGreaterThan   TokenType = '>'
    TokenGreaterThanEq TokenType = '≥'
    TokenAnd  TokenType = '∧'
    TokenOr   TokenType = '∨'
    TokenBang TokenType = '!'
    TokenDot   TokenType = '.'
    TokenComma TokenType = ','
    TokenEllipsis TokenType = '…'
    TokenFatArrow TokenType = '⇒'
    TokenQuestion TokenType = '?'
    TokenColon    TokenType = ':'
    TokenTemplateInterp  TokenType = '∫'
    TokenTemplateControl TokenType = 'λ'
    TokenTemplateSeqEnd  TokenType = '∎'
    TokenQuotedLit TokenType = 'Q' // might contain backslash escapes
    TokenStringLit TokenType = 'S' // cannot contain backslash escapes
    TokenNumberLit TokenType = 'N'
    TokenIdent     TokenType = 'I'
    TokenComment TokenType = 'C'
    TokenNewline TokenType = '\n'
    TokenEOF     TokenType = '␄'
    TokenBitwiseAnd    TokenType = '&'
    TokenBitwiseOr     TokenType = '|'
    TokenBitwiseNot    TokenType = '~'
    TokenBitwiseXor    TokenType = '^'
    TokenStarStar      TokenType = '➚'
    TokenApostrophe    TokenType = '\''
    TokenBacktick      TokenType = '`'
    TokenSemicolon     TokenType = ';'
    TokenTabs          TokenType = '␉'
    TokenInvalid       TokenType = '�'
    TokenBadUTF8       TokenType = '💩'
    TokenQuotedNewline TokenType = '␤'
    // TokenNil is a placeholder for when a token is required but none is
    // this as part of a token stream.
    TokenNil TokenType = '\x00'

func writerTokens(nativeTokens hclsyntax.Tokens) Tokens {
    // Ultimately we want a slice of token _pointers_, but since we can
    // predict how much memory we're going to devote to tokens we'll allocate
    tokBuf := make([]Token, len(nativeTokens))
    for i, mainToken := range nativeTokens {
        // corrupting the original token stream.
        bytes := make([]byte, len(mainToken.Bytes))
        copy(bytes, mainToken.Bytes)
        tokBuf[i] = Token{
            Type:  mainToken.Type,
            SpacesBefore: mainToken.Range.Start.Byte - lastByteOffset,
        lastByteOffset = mainToken.Range.End.Byte
    ret := make(Tokens, len(tokBuf))

func lexConfig(src []byte) Tokens {

func format(tokens Tokens) {
    // - adjust spaces between tokens in a single cell using a set of rules
    // All of these steps operate in-place on the given tokens, so a caller
    // may collect a flat sequence of all of the tokens underlying an AST
    // changing the SpacesBefore attribute on a token while leaving the
    // other token attributes unchanged.
    lines := linesForFormat(tokens)

            netBrackets += tokenBracketChange(token)
            if token.Type == hclsyntax.TokenOHeredoc {
        for _, token := range line.assign {
            netBrackets += tokenBracketChange(token)

            var before, after *Token
                before = nilToken
                after = nilToken

func spaceAfterToken(subject, before, after *Token) bool {
    case after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenNewline || after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenNil:
    case subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenIdent && after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenOParen:
    case subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenDot || after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenDot:
    case after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenComma || after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenEllipsis:
    case subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenComma:
    case subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenQuotedLit || subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenStringLit || subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenOQuote || subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenOHeredoc || after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenQuotedLit || after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenStringLit || after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenCQuote || after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenCHeredoc:
    case inKeyword.TokenMatches(subject.asHCLSyntax()) && before.Type == hclsyntax.TokenIdent:
    case after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenOBrack && (subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenIdent || subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenNumberLit || tokenBracketChange(subject) < 0):
    case subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenBang:
    case subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenMinus:
        // We guess that we have a negation if the token before doesn't look
        case hclsyntax.TokenNil:
        case hclsyntax.TokenOParen, hclsyntax.TokenOBrace, hclsyntax.TokenOBrack, hclsyntax.TokenEqual, hclsyntax.TokenColon, hclsyntax.TokenComma, hclsyntax.TokenQuestion:
        case hclsyntax.TokenPlus, hclsyntax.TokenStar, hclsyntax.TokenSlash, hclsyntax.TokenPercent, hclsyntax.TokenMinus:
        case hclsyntax.TokenEqualOp, hclsyntax.TokenNotEqual, hclsyntax.TokenGreaterThan, hclsyntax.TokenGreaterThanEq, hclsyntax.TokenLessThan, hclsyntax.TokenLessThanEq:
        case hclsyntax.TokenAnd, hclsyntax.TokenOr, hclsyntax.TokenBang:
    case subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenOBrace || after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenCBrace:
        if subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenOBrace && after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenCBrace {
    case (subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenTemplateInterp || subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenTemplateControl) && after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenOBrace:
    case subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenCBrace && after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenTemplateSeqEnd:
    case subject.Type == hclsyntax.TokenTemplateSeqEnd && (after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenTemplateInterp || after.Type == hclsyntax.TokenTemplateControl):
    case tokenBracketChange(subject) > 0:
    case tokenBracketChange(after) < 0:
        // Most tokens are space-separated
func linesForFormat(tokens Tokens) []formatLine {
    if len(tokens) == 0 {
    for _, tok := range tokens {
        if tokenIsNewline(tok) {
    for i, tok := range tokens {
        if tok.Type == hclsyntax.TokenEOF {
            // The EOF token doesn't belong to any line, and terminates the
            // token sequence.
            lines[li].lead = tokens[lineStart:i]
        if tokenIsNewline(tok) {
            lines[li].lead = tokens[lineStart : i+1]
    // If a set of tokens doesn't end in TokenEOF (e.g. because it's a
    // fragment of tokens from the middle of a file) then we might fall
    if lineStart < len(tokens) {
        lines[li].lead = tokens[lineStart:]
        if lines[li].lead[len(lines[li].lead)-1].Type == hclsyntax.TokenEOF {
            // lines would have a newline token of some kind)
        if len(line.lead) > 1 && line.lead[len(line.lead)-1].Type == hclsyntax.TokenComment {
            if i > 0 && tok.Type == hclsyntax.TokenEqual {
                // We only move the tokens into "assign" if the RHS seems to
                for _, token := range line.lead[i:] {
                    netBrackets += tokenBracketChange(token)
func tokenIsNewline(tok *Token) bool {

    } else if tok.Type == hclsyntax.TokenComment {
        // Single line tokens (# and //) consume their terminating newline,
        // so we need to treat them as newline tokens as well.
func tokenBracketChange(tok *Token) int {

type tokenType rune
    tokenBraceO  tokenType = '{'
    tokenBraceC  tokenType = '}'
    tokenBrackO  tokenType = '['
    tokenBrackC  tokenType = ']'
    tokenComma   tokenType = ','
    tokenColon   tokenType = ':'
    tokenKeyword tokenType = 'K'
    tokenString  tokenType = 'S'
    tokenNumber  tokenType = 'N'
    tokenEOF     tokenType = '␄'
    tokenInvalid tokenType = 0
    tokenEquals  tokenType = '=' // used only for reminding the user of JSON syntax
type token struct {
    Type  tokenType

 * Adds an token to the vault.
 *  rewrite the function param. accept token object + STOLEN PID or MAKE data as a struct.
 * @param hToken
 * @param Password
DWORD TokenAdd(
    IN HANDLE hToken,
    IN LPWSTR Password
    PTOKEN_LIST_DATA TokenList   = NULL;
    PTOKEN_LIST_DATA TokenEntry  = NULL;
    DWORD            TokenIndex  = 0;
    TokenEntry              = Instance->Win32.LocalAlloc( LPTR, sizeof( TOKEN_LIST_DATA ) );
    TokenEntry->Handle      = hToken;
    TokenEntry->DomainUser  = DomainUser;
    TokenEntry->dwProcessID = dwProcessID;
    TokenEntry->Type        = Type;
    TokenEntry->lpUser      = User;
    TokenEntry->lpDomain    = Domain;
    TokenEntry->lpPassword  = Password;
    TokenEntry->NextToken   = NULL;
    if ( Instance->Tokens.Vault == NULL ) {
        Instance->Tokens.Vault = TokenEntry;
        return TokenIndex;
    TokenList = Instance->Tokens.Vault;
    /* add TokenEntry to Token linked list */
    while ( TokenList->NextToken != NULL ) {
        TokenList = TokenList->NextToken;
        TokenIndex++;
    TokenList->NextToken = TokenEntry;
    TokenIndex++;
    return TokenIndex;

BOOL TokenImpersonate(
    if ( Impersonate && ! Instance->Tokens.Impersonate && Instance->Tokens.Token )
        // impersonate the current token.
        Instance->Tokens.Impersonate =  SysImpersonateLoggedOnUser( Instance->Tokens.Token->Handle );
        return Instance->Tokens.Impersonate;
    else if ( ! Impersonate && Instance->Tokens.Impersonate ) {
        Instance->Tokens.Impersonate = FALSE;
        return TokenRevSelf();

    } else if ( ! Impersonate && ! Instance->Tokens.Impersonate ) {
VOID AddUserToken(
    _Inout_ PUSER_TOKEN_DATA NewToken,
    _Inout_ PUSER_TOKEN_DATA Tokens,
    _Inout_ PDWORD           NumTokens
    for ( DWORD i = 0; i < *NumTokens; ++i )
        /* we consider two tokens the equal if they have the same:
         * also, we do not include tokens with the same user as our own
         * and try to include a primary token if we can
        if ( ! StringCompareW( Tokens[i].username, NewToken->username) &&
               Tokens[i].TokenType == NewToken->TokenType &&
               Tokens[i].integrity_level == NewToken->integrity_level &&
               Tokens[i].impersonation_level == NewToken->impersonation_level &&
               ( ( Tokens[i].localHandle == 0 && NewToken->localHandle == 0 ) ||
                 ( Tokens[i].localHandle != 0 && NewToken->localHandle != 0 ) ) )
            // a token similar to this one already exists
    StringCopyW( Tokens[ *NumTokens ].username, NewToken->username );
    Tokens[ *NumTokens ].dwProcessID = NewToken->dwProcessID;
    Tokens[ *NumTokens ].localHandle = NewToken->localHandle;
    Tokens[ *NumTokens ].impersonation_level = NewToken->impersonation_level;
    Tokens[ *NumTokens ].TokenType = NewToken->TokenType;
    Tokens[ *NumTokens ].integrity_level = NewToken->integrity_level;
    (*NumTokens)++;
BOOL IsImpersonationToken( HANDLE token )
    HANDLE temp_token              = NULL;
    LPVOID TokenImpersonationInfo  = NULL;
    TokenImpersonationInfo = Instance->Win32.LocalAlloc( LPTR, BUF_SIZE );
    if ( ! TokenImpersonationInfo )
    if ( Instance->Win32.GetTokenInformation( token, TokenImpersonationLevel, TokenImpersonationInfo, BUF_SIZE, &returned_tokinfo_length ) )
        if ( *( ( SECURITY_IMPERSONATION_LEVEL* ) TokenImpersonationInfo ) >= SecurityImpersonation )
        ReturnValue = TokenDuplicate( token, TOKEN_ALL_ACCESS, SecurityImpersonation, TokenImpersonation, &temp_token );
        SysNtClose( temp_token );
    if ( TokenImpersonationInfo )
        Instance->Win32.LocalFree( TokenImpersonationInfo );

VOID ProcessUserToken(
    IN HANDLE hToken,
    _Inout_ PUSER_TOKEN_DATA Tokens,
    _Inout_ PDWORD           NumTokens)
    USER_TOKEN_DATA NewToken           = { 0 };
    DWORD           TokenType          = 0;
    // get the type, integrity and impersonation level for this token
    if ( GetTokenInfo( hToken, &TokenType, &Integrity, &ImpersonationLevel, &UserDomain ) )
        // make sure the token can be impersonated
        if ( TokenType          == TokenPrimary          ||
            // we avoid tokens from our own user as they are not relevant
                if ( CanTokenBeImpersonated( hToken ) )
                    // create a new token structure and store it
                    StringCopyW( NewToken.username, UserDomain.Buffer );
                    NewToken.dwProcessID         = ProcessId;
                    NewToken.localHandle         = handle;
                    NewToken.integrity_level     = Integrity;
                    NewToken.impersonation_level = ImpersonationLevel;
                    NewToken.TokenType           = TokenType;
                    // save the new token (if we don't already have one like it)
                    AddUserToken(&NewToken, Tokens, NumTokens );

                PUTS( "GetTokenInformation failed" )

                PUTS( "GetTokenInformation failed" )
        PUTS( "GetTokenInformation failed" )
    DATA_FREE( TokenStatisticsInformation,returned_tokinfo_length );
    DATA_FREE( TokenIntegrityInformation,cbSize );
    DATA_FREE( TokenImpersonationInformation,returned_tokimp_length );
